                      <div data-reactid="656">
                       This is the bottom story of our house by the beach in Playa del Rey. There is amazing light and north, south, and east views. The house is walking distance to town and the beach and 5 miles to LAX. There is lots of parking. You have your own entrance.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="657">
                       Wake up with the beautiful, warm Southern California sunrise peeking through the trees. The house is on a hill above the beach. There is a yard, outdoor eating area, and little nooks for peaceful relaxation or a cup of coffee. It is a spacious one bedroom with a built in desk. There isn't a kitchen but there is a kitchen space with a refrigerator, stocked Keurig coffee maker, convection oven, water boiler and microwave as well as kitchen supplies and utensils. The space has beautiful light and ocean breezes. It is close to LAX, the beach and all west side Los Angeles locations.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="658">
                       Playa del Rey is Los Angeles's quietest little beach town. We are up on the hill above the town and the beach. The neighborhood is nice and quiet with plenty of street parking and also driveway parking. It's a great walking neighborhood with views up and down the coast from every corner. The neighborhood is on a hill so might not be best for older people to walk around. Guests have their own private entrance but it requires going up stairs from the bottom of the property.
                      </div>

We never cooked while we were there, surprisingly we were gone a lot, but the place has all of the appropriate things you would need to cook. This place is very close to the airport, which was nice for us to be able to get to and from with three kids in tow but you can hear the planes pretty well. Luckily we are not light sleepers at night so this wasn't really a big issue for us. You are in the middle of the LA area staying here so you can get to and from things very easily. We were at Disneyland one day and Malibu the next. Overall our stay was nice and comfortable. </p><span data-reactid="913">Erica</span><span data-reactid="914">2015-05-27T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                       <li data-reactid="915"><p data-reactid="916">What a great adventure Playa del Rey! I arrived late on a Friday evening and after calling Rebecca (the local host and all around great resource), she invited me to join her for dinner if I was hungry. I felt at home immediately because of Rebecca's welcoming spirit. Making reservations and ironing out the details were easy with Shelly before we arrived, so there was nothing to do but arrive and have fun. Safety is a huge issue with me and this is a very secure condo, from the 24 hour guard at the entrance/exit, to the keyed entry from the outdoors into the building to the locks on the unit, it was secure. The condo is on the second floor and looks out over the pool and hot tub where some of the residents gather at night and visit. Inside the condo, it is obvious that Shelly is a world traveler and the unit is tastefully decorated and welcoming. The hard wood floors and the warm area rugs were great for my sons to lay on and watch tv or just crash for the day. The TV has Direct TV so there was plenty to watch at night. The kitchen is well stocked and is very much like being at home in your own kitchen. Rebecca brought over some eggs and orange juice and there was plenty to munch on and enjoy. Nearby are several smaller groceries, but just over the hill and up the street a bit is a Ralph's which was easy to pick up some supplies. The pool is clean and inviting. The boys loved swimming because most of the time, they were the only ones in the water. It is a large pool and has two hot tubs to relax. There were also tennis courts behind the building. Our parking space in the garage was steps from the lower entry into the building. We ran into several other folks in the garage coming in and out and it was very much like a small town atmosphere. Lots of hello's. There was plenty of sleeping room for all of us and the master has a private bath. If I could of brought home any part of the condo, it would of been the shower (and Rebecca, she would be a great neighbor anywhere). It is like standing in the rain forest and is perfect. There was also some liquid soaps and shampoos which made it easier to check our luggage flying because those supplies were already on site. This is a great location, we went to Hollywood one night, Beverly Hills, Disneyland, the beach, Brentwood, Chinatown, Venice Beach, and to a Dodger's game and getting to the freeways was easy and other than a few slow spots, we had no trouble. In my final words, Shelley, thank you for letting us stay in your wonderful home and thank you Rebecca for not only being our host next door, but being a wonderful person to us all!! </p><span data-reactid="917">Steve</span><span data-reactid="918">2014-06-30T00:00:00Z</span></li>

Accommodation was clean and very comfortable. Rebecca, the concierge, was helpful and friendly. With our daughter at LMU, we will stay here again. </p><span data-reactid="921">Missy</span><span data-reactid="922">2014-08-25T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                     <div data-reactid="1335">
                      <div data-reactid="1336">
                       With breathtaking views of the Pacific Ocean from Palos Verdes to Catalina Island to Malibu, this cozy oceanfront beach retreat, which sleeps up to 8, is yours to enjoy for a great family vacation, a romantic getaway or corporate/executive rental
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1337">
                       Our recently remodeled 4 bedroom, 2 bath quaint beach duplex has all the amenities you need to settle right in and feel ‘at home’. With a total of 1500 sq ft, this upper floor unit can comfortably accommodate two families. We prefer children over the age of 5 for the consideration of our lower unit guests. Take your pick of the huge 500 sq ft master bedroom with king size sleigh bed and private en suite bathroom with double vanity and laundry, the Tommy Bahama room with 4 poster queen bed, the Mermaid room with a queen bed or the surfer bunk bed room with 2 twins and 1 full bed for the kids. All bedrooms have new mattresses and quality linens plus ipod clock radios. The gourmet kitchen is fully equipped with dishes and all the cookware you need to prepare a family meal or a gourmet feast with bar seating, a fold out dining room table or dine al fresco at the picnic table outside with seating for 8. Enjoy morning coffee or a glass of wine at sunset from the comfortable balcony filled with rattan &amp; bamboo furniture, flowers and a BBQ. After a long, peaceful day at the beach, relax in front of the 2 flat screen TV’s, one in the living room (52” with DVD, CD, surround sound and Ipod dock) and one in the master bedroom (47”). Just relax and rejuvenate every day as you watch sailboats drift by and dolphins play in the surf. Enjoy long walks along the beach and swim and play in the Pacific Ocean steps out your front door. Take a yoga class on the beach while watching and listening to the sound of the calming ocean waves, or take an easy bike ride to Manhattan Beach or Marina del Rey. Watch the sunset after a perfect day at the beach or walk down the street to enjoy one of the many local restaurants. Sleep peacefully to the sound of the ocean waves. Close to the many attractions in Los Angeles, enjoy a day of exploring and sightseeing. Los Angeles Intl airport is 6 miles away. You will be only 4 miles to Marina del Rey and Venice Beach or 6 miles to Manhattan Beach, 6 miles to Santa Monica, 15 miles to Hollywood, 20 miles to downtown L.A., 24 miles to Malibu, 35 miles to Disneyland and Knotts Berry Farm or 25 miles to Universal Studios, and a 90 minute ferry ride to Catalina Island. Whether you are interested in a family getaway with the kids, family reunion or a romantic quiet rendezvous at the beach, we look forward to hearing from you so that we may share our little piece of ‘paradise’ with you. While we love families/gatherings, we do not allow large groups or parties:)
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1338">
                       Playa del Rey is a sleepy little beach community known for it’s solitude and ‘small town’ feel. A hidden gem and favorite for L.A. locals since it hasn't changed much in the last 30 years. The beaches never get crowded and there are very few tourists, so if you are looking for a great quiet and family oriented area, you've found your retreat!
                      </div>
